TABLE S4: 3D7 vs HB3 Competitive Genomic Hybridization Data
Bozdech & Llinas et al.

This table contains all of the intensity data from competitive genomic hybridizations of genomic  
DNA derived from the 3D7 and HB3 strains of P. falciparum. The averaged intensities from three
microarray hybridization experiments are listed.  A %3D7 intensity in the HB3 channel 
of '-1' indicates that signal in these spots for one or both of the strains was below background.
Strains used in this study were obtained from the Malaria Resource Center (MR4).

Column 1: Oligonucleotide ID
Column 2: PlasmoDB ID
Column 3: PlasmoDB Manual annotation 
Column 4: Averaged normalized intensity for strain 3D7
Column 5: Averaged normalized intensity for strain HB3
Column 6: % of 3D7 intensity in the HB3 channel
